A BOOK OF THE VALUATIONS Of all the Ecclesiastical Preferments IN England and
Wales; Entitled NOMINA and VALORES omnium and singulorum Archiepiscopatuum,
Episcopatuum, Archidiaconat', Decanat', Praebendarum, Ecclesiarumque paroch'
infra Regnum ac Dominia Angliae, ac omnium altarum Promotionum quarumcunque
spiritualium infra eadem, quae ad solutionem decimae partis earund' Dom' Regi
and Reginae nuper tenebantur.

Printed in the Year 1680.

Comitat' ANGLIAE.
Bedford. 1. Berk. 6. Buck. 12. Villa Calesiae. 19. Cantabrig. 21. Cestrens.
28. Cornub. 31. Cumberl. 38. Devon. 45. Dorc. 63. Dunelm. 73. Eborac. 78.
Essex. 96. Gloucest. 111. Hartf. 122. Hereford. 127. Huntingt. 134. Kanc. 138.
Lancast. 153. Leicestr. 154. Lincoln. 162. Civitas London. 187. Middlesex. 194.
Norfolc. 196. Northampt. 223. Nottingham. 234. Oxon. 241. Richmond Archidiac.
248. Rutland. 252. Salop. 255. Somerset. 261. Southampt. 279. Stafford. 289.
Suffolc. 294. Surrey 312. Sussex. 316. Warwic. 329. Wigorn. 335. Wilt. 341.
